msg:Nestled in the heart of Yiwu, Expo City Hotel offers a delightful stay for both business and leisure travelers. From the moment I stepped into the lobby, I was greeted with warmth and hospitality by the attentive staff. The hotel's modern and elegant design creates a welcoming ambiance that immediately puts you at ease.

The rooms at Expo City Hotel are spacious, well-appointed, and meticulously clean. I appreciated the attention to detail, from the comfortable bedding to the thoughtful amenities provided. The panoramic views of the city from my room were simply breathtaking, especially during sunrise and sunset.

One of the highlights of my stay was the dining experience at the hotel's restaurant. The menu offered a diverse selection of both local and international cuisine, prepared with fresh ingredients and expertly presented. The breakfast buffet was particularly impressive, featuring an array of delicious options to suit every palate.

The hotel's convenient location near Yiwu International Trade City and other attractions made it easy for me to explore the city. Additionally, the efficient transportation services offered by the hotel ensured seamless travel throughout my stay.

Overall, my experience at Expo City Hotel was nothing short of exceptional. The combination of luxurious accommodations, impeccable service, and prime location make it the perfect choice for travelers visiting Yiwu. I look forward to returning to Expo City Hotel for my future visits to the city.

msg:Booked a hotel for the Yiwu exhibition. Yiwu International Expo Center is 200 meters away. It is quite convenient.
The hotel gym facilities are basically complete. Since few people use it, it is very comfortable.
In terms of catering, the breakfast is quite satisfactory. But there are not many good restaurants around.
The above are good aspects.
In terms of service and hygiene, there are some unsatisfactory aspects.
First of all, for an Expo Center hotel, when I asked the staff at the hotel entrance how to get to the exhibition hall, the reply I gave was "I don't know". Then, when I went back to the hotel lobby to ask the concierge, the reply I gave was "next door". It didn't say whether it was left, right or where. Although it was only more than 200 meters, this way of reply was unqualified.
Secondly, the most excessive thing was that the welcome fruit was moldy, which was extremely scary! This has already involved the level of food safety. Therefore, I was not very satisfied.
